              (0): Sequential(
                (0): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(5, 5), stride=(1, 1), padding=(2, 2), groups=128, bias=False)
                (1): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.01, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
                (2): ReLU()
              )
              (1): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
              (2): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.01, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
              (3): ReLU()
            )
          )
          (1): Conv2d(128, 1, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        )
        (offset): Sequential(
          (0): Sequential(
            (0): Sequential(
              (0): Sequential(
                (0): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(5, 5), stride=(1, 1), padding=(2, 2), groups=128, bias=False)
                (1): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.01, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
                (2): ReLU()

              (1): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)
              (2): BatchNorm2d(128, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.01, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
              (3): ReLU()
            )
          )
          (1): Conv2d(128, 2, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (semantic_loss): DeepLabCE(
    (criterion): CrossEntropyLoss()
  )
  (center_loss): MSELoss()
  (offset_loss): L1Loss()
